# How to install and run MLCFlow (on Expanse) [Part V]

${MLC_PYTHON_BIN} -m pip install -r ${MLC_TMP_CURRENT_SCRIPT_PATH}/requirements.txt ${PIP_EXTRA}

MLC_PYTHON_BIN=${MLC_PYTHON_BIN_WITH_PATH:-python3}
